=== Af-Soomaali, Fasalka 3aad ===
Immisa jir ayaa uu ahaa Nebi Muxammed ( NNKH ) markii uu aabbihiis dhintay ? Shanta Tiir Islaam Baro shanta tiir ee Islaamka . Maryan aabbaheed iyo hooyadeed maxaa ay ku yidhaahdeen Sahra ? Markii la gaadhay wakhtigii la goyn lahaa , ayey ku heshiiyeen in ay beerta u qaybiyaan saddex meelood .

=== Af-Soomaali, Fasalka 4aad ===
